You may own more then one slot at a one time.

update, rules:
- Trooper skills that appear in the 'recruit's description' of a slot that you own may not match those of a different slot that you already own.
Exceptions: This may happen if the 'army links' in each slot are different. This may happen if the owner is useing the word 'any' as one of the two trooper skill.
